Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele; puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment: si revenra a son leu maintenant; et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	If the dislocation is in the knee, it is necessary to treat its appearance. The patient should be placed on their side with the healthy leg above the injured one, then tie the ligament at the root of the thigh and the one behind the angle. Then stretch the ligament towards the angle and towards the strength; have other assistants grasp the patient's arms, embrace the large ligament of the injured thigh, and extend it to a different form; it will return to its place now, and this method of dislocation is lighter than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres; puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc; puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	And if you cannot hold it in the manner we have said, then it is necessary that you tie both feet of the patient together with a strong soft bandage on both heels and both knees, and let the leg of the patient be extended two fingers more than the other; then hang it over a post, and let it reach two arms' length above the ground; then command the minister to embrace the top of the thigh, and have other ministers hanging with the patient, who embrace the thigh, for the joint now comes back naturally.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi; puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme; et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	And when the dislocation is external, if the patient lies down as we have said in the case of stiffness, then tighten the bandage properly on the leg of the patient, also on the side; then place two hot coals, one at the top and one at the foot, and insert a hot coal between the thighs of the patient, forming it; and place moist towels around, so that they do not hurt the patient, then extend each minister towards him, and make them put the dislocation back in its place with their hands.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, that is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If it does not return, place it on a table and press it as we have said in the previous section, and lay the patient on their healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit; et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And when dislocation occurs, it is necessary to stretch the affected leg forcefully, as I have said, and alleviate the patient's pain by applying pressure with one hand, then stretching it downwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches; et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table; et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve; et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And if the dislocation is towards the outside, it is not necessary to stretch the affected leg downwards or raise it up, but rather, it should remain in the same position as when the hip was dislocated outward; just as we have said, gently pressing it down on both hips, and then extending the leg as mentioned before. It must be pressed against the joint on a table. And this will be effective when the patient extends their legs, and they are even. Then, tighten the cuffs, apply a splint, and wrap a bandage around it, so that the hip does not move. Let it rest for three or four days, then untie it and apply a splint; and if you see that they are even, just as before, leave the bandage on for three more days, after which gently make the patient walk, until the limb is healed.
de la dislocation dou genoil	From the dislocation of the knee.
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The limb is dislocated in three ways: internally, externally, and posteriorly; but not anteriorly.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez; et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez; puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement; et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And the signs are that you command the patient to bend his leg at the knee, and if he does not flex at the knee, know that it is dislocated; and the restoration of all is that you make the patient sit straight, and extend his leg if he can, and place his face on your hand, and place his foot on yours. Then take his knee in your palms and pull between your fingers, then bend both sides of the knee joint; and another assistant extends his foot, until the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that it flexes slightly at the knee. And apply a poultice, and keep the leg extended at the knee, and bind them together firmly for three or four days, then release them; and let not the patient move about, until the limb is comforted.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not at all straight, apply firm extension as we have said in the treatment of the spine, as long as it is healthy.
de la dislocation dou talon	On the dislocation of the talus bone.
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The talus bone is neither perfectly aligned nor fully dislocated, being both inside and outside its proper position.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen, and there is tenderness in the area where it is dislocated; its reduction is gentle, and one should gently extend their hand towards the affected side when it is slightly dislocated.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is dislocated from all sides, you should make the patient lie straight, and hold the leg away from the body with the aid of another person, above the ankle; then take the foot in your right hand, and twice stretch it towards yourself, then upwards, and nicely pull the foot upwards; do this twice more, as we have said, by bending and stretching the foot; if it returns, that is good; if not, repeat the process, because it will return; and if it cannot return like that, make the patient lie on his back on the ground, and insert a firm stick in the ground between his legs, and wrap the sheets around him so he does not hurt himself; then have each minister hold the thigh, and others stretch the foot towards his hands or the knee, so it lies above the ankle; then each minister should stretch equally, and the stick should be placed between the patient's legs to keep him still when they stretch him; then place the mirrors equally on both sides of the dislocation, and another minister hold the healthy leg from below, and the dislocation will return properly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when the wound is healed, apply a poultice and compress it, stretch the limb, and bind the foot to the leg, keeping the shoes on behind the ankle so the ligaments do not become too tight; then leave it for two or three days, and if the stretching is gone, untie it on the third day or fourth, and the patient must walk for four days; and if he continues beyond that time, it is not fortunate for him to heal completely.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if abscesses form, it is necessary to soothe them, as we have said elsewhere, while they are fresh.
des dois	Of the two (parts/sides)
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When both (sides) are dislocated, if they need to be rightly extended without effort, it is a light thing.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any other part of the back or foot, it is necessary that you make the patient lie on their back or on a table completely straight, and place your foot on what opens from these joints, then press with your foot's form until it returns; and when it is even and opens nothing, put a table under the sole of the foot at the level of two joints, then stretch it strongly, and leave it for three days, then release it; and let it rest until it is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	From wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound occurs with dislocation and it is desired to restore it, it often happens that the patient dies: if you are not careful in treating it, since you lack knowledge of this art and have not practiced it for a long time, and if you are not merciful and slow, then do not be bold; at the beginning, use hot apithic applications on the abscess, and leave the patient in God's hands, if you see no hope of recovery; but when there is hope, immediately reposition the limb to its correct place, so that the abscess does not return; and while the limb is dislocated, apply hot apithic applications to the abscess, treat the wound as appropriate from drying agents, and if it is a fracture with small broken bones, reduce them, and follow what we have said about simple diseases; and beware of entering a path of fear, as I have said, for this is your salvation according to your Creator, and for the knowledge of your arms and body.
Amen	Indeed, here is the line
